FROM [AbpBackgroundJobs] AS [a]
WHERE [a].[IsAbandoned] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [a].[NextTryTime] <= @__Now_0
ORDER BY [a].[Priority] DESC, [a].[TryCount], [a].[NextTryTime]
